CA_001

CoApplicant Mandatory Check

👤 Applies: Application
📋 Scheme: All
Summary
Co-applicant or guarantor must be present
  1. IF co_applicant_count ≥ 1 OR guarantor_count ≥ 1 -> PASS. ELSE -> FAIL.
Logic Table
ConditionOutcome
co_applicant_count >= 1 OR guarantor_count >= 1✓ PASS
Otherwise✗ FAIL
Decision Tree

CA_002

Married Applicant Spouse Check

👤 Applies: Applicant
📋 Scheme: All
🏷 Constitutions: BANK SALARIED | CASH SALARY | SEP - ITR | SEP - ASSESSED INCOME | BUSINESS | SENP - ITR | SENP - ASSESSED INCOME | SENP- NO ITR
Summary
Married applicant must have spouse as co-applicant; missing spouse is L5 deviation
  1. IF Applicant.marital_status != 'M' -> PASS. ELIF Applicant.marital_status == 'M' AND Has_Spouse_CoApplicant == TRUE -> PASS. ELIF product is identified -> raise product-wise L5 deviation for missing spouse co-applicant. ELSE -> FAIL.
Grouped Deviation View
current_deal_product_name == 'HFL'
HFL: 6827
current_deal_product_name == 'NRP'
NRP: 6828
current_deal_product_name == 'LAP'
LAP: 6829
current_deal_product_name == 'PC'
PC: 6830
Deviation Names (Omnifin)
Omnifin deviation nameDeviation codes
Spouse not on loan structure6827 | 6828 | 6829 | 6830
Logic Table
ConditionOutcome
Applicant.marital_status != 'M'✓ PASS
Applicant.marital_status == 'M' AND Has Spouse CoApplicant == TRUE✓ PASS
current_deal_product_name == 'HFL'⚠ Deviate (6827)
current_deal_product_name == 'NRP'⚠ Deviate (6828)
current_deal_product_name == 'LAP'⚠ Deviate (6829)
current_deal_product_name == 'PC'⚠ Deviate (6830)
Otherwise✗ FAIL

Calculations
Has Spouse CoApplicant (Application)
Checks if any co-applicant has relationship = SPOUSE with the applicant. Returns TRUE/FALSE at Application level.
COUNT(co_applicants[*] WHERE relationship_with_applicant == 'SPOUSE') >= 1

Policy Ref: Pg 6, Sec 3.2 — Married applicant spouse as co-applicant

AE_001

Bureau Score Check

👤 Applies: Applicant | Co-applicant | Guarantor
📋 Scheme: All
🏷 Constitutions: BANK SALARIED | CASH SALARY | SEP - ITR | SEP - ASSESSED INCOME | BUSINESS | SENP - ITR | SENP - ASSESSED INCOME | SENP- NO ITR | HOMEMAKER | NOT WORKING / NON SALARIED | OTHER
Summary
Bureau score >= 650 or NTC (-1 to 18); otherwise product-wise deviation
  1. If CRIF score >= 650 -> PASS. If NTC (-1 to 18) -> PASS. If score is below 650 and not NTC and product is identified -> Deviate using existing product-wise bureau score deviation codes. ELSE -> FAIL.

AE_002

Bureau Overdue Check

👤 Applies: Applicant | Co-applicant
📋 Scheme: All
🏷 Constitutions: BANK SALARIED | CASH SALARY | SEP - ITR | SEP - ASSESSED INCOME | BUSINESS | SENP - ITR | SENP - ASSESSED INCOME | SENP- NO ITR | HOMEMAKER | NOT WORKING / NON SALARIED | OTHER
Summary
Bureau overdue check for Applicant/Co-applicant
  1. IF Applicant/Co-applicant.bureau_overdue_amount == 0 -> PASS. ELIF bureau_overdue_amount ≤ 10000 -> raise deviation (HFL->6411, NRP->6412, LAP->6413, PC->6422). ELIF bureau_overdue_amount -> 10000 -> raise deviation (HFL->6399, NRP->6400, LAP->6401, PC->6410). ELSE PASS.
Grouped Deviation View
Applicant/Co-applicant.bureau_overdue_amount <= 10000
HFL: 6411NRP: 6412LAP: 6413PC: 6422
Applicant/Co-applicant.bureau_overdue_amount >= 10000
HFL: 6399NRP: 6400LAP: 6401PC: 6410
Deviation Names (Omnifin)
Omnifin deviation nameDeviation codes
Overdue/DPD/Suit Filed/Willful Default seen in Bureau for any live/closed loans/credit card and where overdue amount does not exceed Rs. 10,0006411 | 6412 | 6413 | 6422
Overdue/DPD/Suit Filed/Willful Default seen in Bureau for any live/closed loans/credit card and where overdue amount exceeds Rs. 10,0006399 | 6400 | 6401 | 6410

Applicant/Co-applicant.bureau_overdue_amount >= 10000 AND current_deal_product_name == 'LAP'⚠ Deviate (6401)
Applicant/Co-applicant.bureau_overdue_amount >= 10000 AND current_deal_product_name == 'PC'⚠ Deviate (6410)
Otherwise✓ PASS

LA_001

Minimum Loan Amount

👤 Applies: Application
📋 Scheme: All
Summary
Min loan amount Rs. 1 Lakh for HOME LOAN TOP UP/LAP TOP UP; Rs. 5 Lakh for listed other schemes including LAP BALANCE TRANSFER TOP UP
  1. If Scheme is one of ('HOME LOAN TOP UP', 'LAP TOP UP') and Loan Amount >= 1 lakh -> PASS. If Scheme is one of ('HOME LOAN TOP UP', 'LAP TOP UP') and Loan Amount < 1 lakh -> FAIL. If Scheme is one of ('HOME LOAN', 'HOME IMPROVEMENT LOAN', 'HOME LOAN BALANCE TRANSFER', 'HOME LOAN CONSTRUCTION', 'HOME LOAN FOR WOMEN', 'PRADHAN MANTRI AWAS YOJANA', 'LAP BALANCE TRANSFER', 'LAP BALANCE TRANSFER TOP UP', 'LAP COMMERCIAL', 'LAP INDUSTRIAL', 'LAP LOAN FOR WOMEN', 'LAP RESIDENTIAL', 'NON RESIDENTIAL PURCHASE', 'PC LOAN FOR WOMEN', 'PC NORMAL') and Loan Amount >= 5 lakh -> PASS. If Scheme is one of the 5 lakh minimum schemes and Loan Amount < 5 lakh -> Deviate (HFL->6791, NRP->6792, LAP->6793, PC->6794).

BR_002

Cash Salaried Eligibility

👤 Applies: Application
📋 Scheme: All
Summary
Cash Salaried: only HL and Top-Up
  1. Cash Salaried (CASH SALARY) Eligibility: Allowed Schemes: HOME LOAN, HOME IMPROVEMENT LOAN, HOME LOAN BALANCE TRANSFER, HOME LOAN CONSTRUCTION, HOME LOAN FOR WOMEN, PRADHAN MANTRI AWAS YOJANA, PC LOAN FOR WOMEN, PC NORMAL, HOME LOAN TOP UP, LAP TOP UP. All other schemes -> FAIL.

EV_002

Salaried Total Experience

👤 Applies: Applicant | Co-applicant
📋 Scheme: All
🏷 Constitutions: BANK SALARIED | CASH SALARY
Summary
Salaried total experience for Applicant/Co-applicant
  1. IF Income_Provided_Flag == 'N' -> SKIP (N/A — income not considered). Home Loan category: ≥ 24 months -> PASS. 12 to 23 months -> DEVIATE L3 (Regional Manager). < 12 months -> DEVIATE L4 (Zonal Head). Non-Home Loan category: ≥ 36 months -> PASS. 12 to 35 months -> DEVIATE L3 (Regional Manager). < 12 months -> DEVIATE L4 (Zonal Head).

MI_002

Minimum Co-applicant Income

👤 Applies: Co-applicant
📋 Scheme: All
🏷 Constitutions: BANK SALARIED | CASH SALARY | SEP - ITR | SEP - ASSESSED INCOME | BUSINESS | SENP - ITR | SENP - ASSESSED INCOME | SENP- NO ITR
Summary
Additional Co-applicant direct monthly income (Net Income) >= Rs. 5,000/month
  1. IF Co-applicant.Income_Provided_Flag == 'N' -> SKIP (income not considered for Co-applicant). ELIF Net Income direct monthly income >= 5000 -> PASS. ELSE -> FAIL (additional Co-applicant income below Rs. 5,000/month floor).

Net Income >= 5000✓ PASS
Otherwise✗ FAIL

Calculations
Net Income (Per_Person)
Role-wise direct monthly income from INP_104 monthly_income_raw. Replaces component-derived recognized income in V2.
IF Co-applicant.monthly_income_raw == None THEN 0 ELSE Co-applicant.monthly_income_raw
Income Provided Flag (Per_Person)
Derived income participation flag: 'Y' if person has non-null non-zero monthly income, else 'N'
IF Co-applicant.monthly_income_raw > 0 THEN 'Y' ELSE 'N'

  1. IF Application Segment is NOT one of ('BANK SALARIED', 'SEP - ITR', 'SENP - ITR') -> PASS (N/A). No deviation bands for this rule. Hard-fail slabs: <=30L max 90%, >30L to <=50L max 80%, >50L max 75%.

LTV_003

LTV — Plot Loan

👤 Applies: Application
📋 Scheme: PC LOAN FOR WOMEN | PC NORMAL
Summary
Plot loan: slab-wise L3/L4/L5 bands capped by hard fail caps 90%/80%/75%
  1. PC scheme LTV uses property_realizable_value as denominator. Deviation bands are applied inside each hard-fail slab: <=30L base 70%, L3 up to 75%, L4 up to 80%, L5 up to 90%; >30L to <=50L base 70%, L3 up to 75%, L4 up to 80%; >50L base 70%, L3 up to 75%. Anything above the slab cap is FAIL.

LTV_004

LTV — NON RESIDENTIAL PURCHASE

👤 Applies: Application
📋 Scheme: NON RESIDENTIAL PURCHASE
Summary
Commercial LTV: 70% municipal / 60% outside
  1. IF is_within_municipal_limits == TRUE AND LTV_only_current_deal ≤ 70 -> PASS. ELIF is_within_municipal_limits == FALSE AND LTV_only_current_deal ≤ 60 -> PASS. ELIF is_within_municipal_limits == TRUE AND LTV_only_current_deal ≤ 75 -> raise deviation (HFL->6363, NRP->6364, LAP->6365, PC->6374). ELIF is_within_municipal_limits == FALSE AND LTV_only_current_deal ≤ 65 -> raise deviation (HFL->6363, NRP->6364, LAP->6365, PC->6374). ELIF is_within_municipal_limits == TRUE AND LTV_only_current_deal ≤ 80 -> raise deviation (HFL->6483, NRP->6484, LAP->6485, PC->6494). ELIF is_within_municipal_limits == FALSE AND LTV_only_current_deal ≤ 70 -> raise deviation (HFL->6483, NRP->6484, LAP->6485, PC->6494). ELSE -> raise deviation (HFL->6235, NRP->6289, LAP->6253, PC->6307).

LTV_007

LTV — Top-Up Combined

👤 Applies: Application
📋 Scheme: HOME LOAN TOP UP | LAP TOP UP
Summary
Top-Up combined LTV: 75% HL / 65% Non-HL, L3/L4/L5 deviations
  1. IF current_deal_scheme_name == 'HOME LOAN TOP UP' AND LTV_including_current_deal_and_base_deal ≤ 75 -> PASS. ELIF same scheme AND LTV_including_current_deal_and_base_deal ≤ 80 -> raise deviation (HFL->6363, NRP->6364, LAP->6365, PC->6374). ELIF same scheme AND LTV_including_current_deal_and_base_deal ≤ 85 -> raise deviation (HFL->6483, NRP->6484, LAP->6485, PC->6494). ELIF same scheme AND LTV_including_current_deal_and_base_deal -> 85 -> raise deviation (HFL->6235, NRP->6289, LAP->6253, PC->6307). ELIF current_deal_scheme_name IN (LAP TOP UP/LAP BALANCE TRANSFER TOP UP) AND LTV_including_current_deal_and_base_deal ≤ 65 -> PASS. ELIF same schemes AND LTV_including_current_deal_and_base_deal ≤ 70 -> raise deviation (HFL->6363, NRP->6364, LAP->6365, PC->6374). ELIF same schemes AND LTV_including_current_deal_and_base_deal ≤ 75 -> raise deviation (HFL->6483, NRP->6484, LAP->6485, PC->6494). ELSE -> raise deviation (HFL->6235, NRP->6289, LAP->6253, PC->6307).

UC_001

UC Min Completion %

👤 Applies: Application
📋 Scheme: HOME LOAN BALANCE TRANSFER | LAP BALANCE TRANSFER | LAP BALANCE TRANSFER TOP UP
Summary
UC property in BT schemes requires L6 deviation
  1. Applicable only for BT schemes: HOME LOAN BALANCE TRANSFER, LAP BALANCE TRANSFER, LAP BALANCE TRANSFER TOP UP. IF Property Under Construction = FALSE -> PASS. ELSE -> raise L6 deviation using existing product-wise codes (HFL->6807, NRP->6808, LAP->6809, PC->6810).

FR_001

FOIR Limit

👤 Applies: Application
📋 Scheme: All
Summary
FOIR limits by direct monthly income slab with deviation tiers
  1. IF Combined_Monthly_Income == 0 -> FAIL. IF Combined_Monthly_Income ≤ 20000: FOIR_Percentage ≤ 40 -> PASS; ≤ 45 -> raise deviation (HFL->6363, NRP->6364, LAP->6365, PC->6374); ≤ 50 -> raise deviation (HFL->6483, NRP->6484, LAP->6485, PC->6494); ELSE -> raise deviation (HFL->6235, NRP->6289, LAP->6253, PC->6307). ELIF Combined_Monthly_Income ≤ 35000: FOIR_Percentage ≤ 45 -> PASS; ≤ 50 -> raise deviation (HFL->6363, NRP->6364, LAP->6365, PC->6374); ≤ 55 -> raise deviation (HFL->6483, NRP->6484, LAP->6485, PC->6494); ELSE -> raise deviation (HFL->6235, NRP->6289, LAP->6253, PC->6307). ELIF Combined_Monthly_Income ≤ 70000: FOIR_Percentage ≤ 50 -> PASS; ≤ 55 -> raise deviation (HFL->6363, NRP->6364, LAP->6365, PC->6374); ≤ 60 -> raise deviation (HFL->6483, NRP->6484, LAP->6485, PC->6494); ELSE -> raise deviation (HFL->6235, NRP->6289, LAP->6253, PC->6307). ELIF Combined_Monthly_Income -> 70000: FOIR_Percentage ≤ 60 -> PASS; ≤ 65 -> raise deviation (HFL->6363, NRP->6364, LAP->6365, PC->6374); ≤ 70 -> raise deviation (HFL->6483, NRP->6484, LAP->6485, PC->6494); ELSE -> raise deviation (HFL->6235, NRP->6289, LAP->6253, PC->6307). ELSE -> FAIL.

Product CategoryApplication
Calculations
Combined Monthly Income (Application)
Combined monthly income = sum of direct role-wise monthly income (Net Income) for Applicant/Co-applicant roles where Income Provided Flag == 'Y'.
SUM(ALL_ROLES.Net Income WHERE Income Provided Flag == 'Y')
FOIR Percentage (Application)
FOIR = (Obligations + EMI) / combined direct monthly income (Combined Monthly Income) x 100.
IF Combined Monthly Income == 0 THEN 0 ELSE (total_existing_obligations + proposed_emi) / Combined Monthly Income * 100

Input Fields

55 active inputs
Only active inputs and calculations are listed here. Active means referenced by an active rule directly or through a calculation used by an active rule.
Calculation Reference 20 active calcs
Net Income (Per_Person)
Role-wise direct monthly income from INP_104 monthly_income_raw. Replaces component-derived recognized income in V2.
IF Role.monthly_income_raw == None THEN 0 ELSE Role.monthly_income_raw
Combined Monthly Income (Application)
Combined monthly income = sum of direct role-wise monthly income (Net Income) for Applicant/Co-applicant roles where Income Provided Flag == 'Y'.
SUM(ALL_ROLES.Net Income WHERE Income Provided Flag == 'Y')
FOIR Percentage (Application)
FOIR = (Obligations + EMI) / combined direct monthly income (Combined Monthly Income) x 100.
IF Combined Monthly Income == 0 THEN 0 ELSE (total_existing_obligations + proposed_emi) / Combined Monthly Income * 100
LTV only current deal (Application)
LTV for current deal only = Loan Amount of Current Deal (including Insurance) / Property Realizable Value × 100
loan_amount_of_current_deal_including_insurance * 100 / property_realizable_value
LTV including current deal and base deal (Application)
Combined LTV for top-up = (Current Deal Loan (incl. Ins) + Base Deal Loan + Base Deal Insurance) / Property Realizable Value × 100
(loan_amount_of_current_deal_including_insurance + loan_amount_of_base_deal + insurance_premium_amount_of_base_deal) * 100 / property_realizable_value
Age At Maturity (Per_Person)
Role age at loan maturity in years. Derived by adding loan tenure (converted from months to years) to age at application (Age).
Age + (tenure_in_months / 12)
Residual Life At Maturity (Application)
Residual life at maturity
estimated_residual_life_years - (tenure_in_months / 12)
Primary Financial Applicant (Application)
Role name with highest direct monthly income (Net Income); tie-breaker: Applicant.
HIGHEST(ALL_ROLES.Net Income, tie_breaker='Applicant')
Application Segment (Application)
Returns customer_constitution_code of the Applicant/Co-applicant role with the highest direct monthly income (Net Income). Applicant preferred on tie. Used as the application-level segment for segment-dependent rule checks.
Primary Financial Applicant.customer_constitution_code
Age (Per_Person)
Age of Role in years at application date
FLOOR((Current_Date - Role.date_of_birth) / 365.25)
Employment Months (Per_Person)
Months in current employment
(Role.bv_employment_years_raw * 12) + Role.bv_employment_months_raw
Same line Business Vintage Months (Per_Person)
Business vintage in months
(Role.bv_employment_years_raw * 12) + Role.bv_employment_months_raw
Residence Duration Months (Per_Person)
Residence duration at current address in months. Computed from raw years and months inputs (INP_095, INP_096). Used by EV_005 to check minimum residence stability threshold.
(Role.residence_years_raw * 12) + Role.residence_months_raw
Income Earner Count (Application)
Count of income earners on deal
COUNT(ALL_ROLES WHERE Income Provided Flag == 'Y')
Cash Salaried Count (Application)
Count of cash salaried income earners
COUNT(ALL_ROLES WHERE customer_constitution_code == 'CASH SALARY' AND Income Provided Flag == 'Y')
Includes Construction (Application)
Returns True if the current deal scheme includes a construction component. Evaluated by checking if the scheme name contains "Construction".
current_deal_scheme_name == "PC LOAN FOR WOMEN" OR current_deal_scheme_name == "PC NORMAL"
Has Spouse CoApplicant (Application)
Checks if any co-applicant has relationship = SPOUSE with the applicant. Returns TRUE/FALSE at Application level.
COUNT(co_applicants[*] WHERE relationship_with_applicant == 'SPOUSE') >= 1
Income Provided Flag (Per_Person)
Derived income participation flag: 'Y' if person has non-null non-zero monthly income, else 'N'
IF Role.monthly_income_raw > 0 THEN 'Y' ELSE 'N'
Any Female Borrower (Application)
Returns TRUE if the applicant or any co-applicant is female.
(Applicant.gender == 'FEMALE') OR (COUNT(co_applicants[*] WHERE gender == 'FEMALE') > 0)
Any Income Provided SE Business Borrower (Application)
Returns TRUE when the Applicant or any Co-applicant has Income Provided Flag = 'Y' and belongs to SEP, SEP_ASSESS, BUSINESS, SELFEMP, SELFEMP_AS, or SELFNOEMP.
(Applicant.Income Provided Flag == 'Y' AND (Applicant.customer_constitution_code == 'SEP - ITR' OR Applicant.customer_constitution_code == 'SEP - ASSESSED INCOME' OR Applicant.customer_constitution_code == 'BUSINESS' OR Applicant.customer_constitution_code == 'SENP - ITR' OR Applicant.customer_constitution_code == 'SENP - ASSESSED INCOME' OR Applicant.customer_constitution_code == 'SENP- NO ITR')) OR (COUNT(co_applicants[*] WHERE Income Provided Flag == 'Y' AND (customer_constitution_code == 'SEP - ITR' OR customer_constitution_code == 'SEP - ASSESSED INCOME' OR customer_constitution_code == 'BUSINESS' OR customer_constitution_code == 'SENP - ITR' OR customer_constitution_code == 'SENP - ASSESSED INCOME' OR customer_constitution_code == 'SENP- NO ITR')) > 0)
